<Review>Appliances are important!  They are what you use every day, and they need to carry the heavy load especially with so many of us working from home now.  So you need a good selection of brands, various price ranges and great service.  Asien's has all that.  But, what really matters is how does the Manager and Staff respond when you need communication and help. Vernon, the Manager, jumped in today because my Salesman had the day off and couldn't troubleshoot for me.  My installer was in the warehouse to pick up my dishwasher, but they couldn't locate it.  Vernon jumped in quickly after I called, determined the issue and solved the problem.  He called my installer to come back to the warehouse, and I am happy to say my new dishwasher is installed.  When installers book out so far,  I couldn't wait until after Thanksgiving for the dishwasher.  My dishwasher was not functioning!  I was impressed that Vernon took decisive action and communicated clearly what he intended to do and how long it would take to get back to me. <review>**Update**
Since my last review I can only add to how impressed I am with service and quality of their water.  They also offer Alkaline water which is what I prefer.

My wife and I had a little girl since our last review and all through those trying months my wife and I were drinking this water.  After our baby was born, we had also used the water for not only our consumption, but also for making our little girl's bottles because of the water's purity.

Overall still the only water we drink and not only is it so much cheaper than buying bottle water but it tastes better and your purchasing from a wonderful family owned business.

*Original Post*
I've been going to Healthy Water for about two months now.  Family owned and how more polite, friendly, and helpful can they be?  I previously used a Brita then PUR filters with my tap water, but that only filtered out some of the particulates in the water.

Healthy water has a top of the line water filtration system that even removes the fluoride amongst many other unwanted contaminants that carbon filters cannot .  The owner explained to me that they perform consistent maintenance to keep their filtration system clean which I can't say for other water stores.  The purity is amazing and the price is right!

My wife who is now six months pregnant loves carbonated water so we use the water with a Soda Stream to make sure she always has the best carbonated water.  I'm writing this review because I am about to head on over and get a refill for my jug and right now I wouldn't be going any place else.  I will try out the alkaline to see if it's worth it.

Five stars.<//review>< pics>

This place and the owners are THE BEST. The coffee options are excellent, baked goods and all food are beyond reproach. < review>
I broke a tooth and the doctor took me in immediately, even though I'd never visited him before.  The tooth needed a crown. He prepared the tooth for the crown on that first visit.-Pain free.  Four days later the crown was in place, looked good and felt good.  Unusual in my experience.
His array of high tech instruments was impressive, including safer, very low energy X-rays and a camera to take photos of teeth from inside a mouth.  From the photos you can get a clear image of the tooth's problems.  I would have liked deeper explanations of why procedures were necessary, and a lower pressure sales pitch.
Dentist and his staff were friendly, helpful, and efficient. The office was a comfortable place to be (given that it was a dentist's). How they handle the insurance issues is yet to be seen.</review>

My very first impression of this company was amazing!! I had lots of flyers and had no idea how to choose a dentist.. all my past dentist were recommended to me. I’m so glad that I found Escondido Family Dental Care through a simple flyer that most people toss! I called many places and was not at all impressed. I had to leave a couple of messages with answering services that really didn’t know basic information like if they accepted my type of insurance and if there was always someone there on Thursdays. However, if those places knew the answers then I would probably never even called this gem!! The person was so helpful and pleasant on the phone and it seemed so simple to answer my questions and fit me in while another place was more than 2 more months in advance to make an appointment for a new patient and one place kept putting me on hold to find an answer to my questions. I came in and even was wondering since I arrived a little too late for my liking that they would ask to reschedule me but again.. they gave me time to fill out the forms and were very easy going. The doctor came up and was so nice introduced himself and told me it would only be a little while longer. I felt right away I was in great hands! The atmosphere was so relaxing and going to the dentist can be dreadful, but I left there feeling confident I made the right choice even though I could’ve probably paid nothing to get a crown fixed by my previous dentist.. once the lady gave me a visual of the crown I currently had and the feeling of the one the dentist recommended. This presentation just made it easier to make my own decision and not just take the word of a professional. The hygienist was very sweet and took time to connect with me and did an amazing job cleaning my teeth! This place is nothing like the outside.. it’s full of wonderful gadgets and the staff know how to do their absolute best to ensure people feel comfortable and welcome. Plus, Dr. Raza is so nice and really is so pleasant and took his time! I even look forward to going back.. not often do I say that about a dental office.< /Text>

< Text>
I cannot say enough good things about Dr. Raza and his staff.

After going to a different place within my husband's Military Concordia network they quoted me roughly 7.5 grand for various dental work. We simply could not afford that with our new house and growing family. This bill was also accompanied by unprofessionalism, high pressure sales tactics and huge wait time.

After seeing his good reviews online we wanted to get a second opinion and see if I needed all that work to begin with (I..uh did, my bad). However the entire experience was a complete opposite. Newer machine made my X-ray's easy. The staff was kind and knowledgeable and I was seen to promptly. After getting a thorough check up they gave me a projected bill. ONE THIRD of what the other place wanted. They offered various payment plans and had very flexible dates for procedures

I just finished a root canal and fillings. I barely felt anything during or after the procedure. The staff and Dr.Raza were so gentle and reassuring. Explaining anything I wanted to know ahead of time, and checked in with me during. I have more dental work to complete including getting wisdom teeth removed. I have full confidence in getting quality work done and plan on taking my twins here for their first dental check up.</Text>

1. Dr. Raza was not willing to "settle" with this - he re-ordered another crown and set me up with another appointment, all to get things done RIGHT (at no extra cost to me). If he had "settled" I probably would have been right back in the dental chair - getting this same crown re-done in 3-5 years.
